BAG MED PA LA MI GNAS

PAR BSKUL BAR SPRO'O, ,BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' BLO GROS MI ZAD PAS
GSOL PA, BCOM LDAN 'DAS, BDAG NI SEMS CAN THAMS CAD LA ZAD MI
SHES PA'I DBYINGS KYI DON MTHONG

BAR BSTAN PAR SPRO'O, ,BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' ZLA 'OD DBUS GSOL PA,
BCOM LDAN 'DAS, BDAG NI SEMS CAN THAMS CAD BLA NA MED PA'I BDE
BA'I SBYIN PA BGYI BAR SPRO'O ZHES

BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' DE DAG SO SO NAS DAM BCAS SO, ,BYANG CHUB
YONGS SU BRGYAN CING, SEMS CAN THAMS CAD LA PHAN ZHING BDE BA
DANG, SANGS RGYAS KYI BKA' DRIN DRAN ZHING,

SANGS RGYAS KYI BKA' DRIN BSAB PA'I PHYIR, STAN LAS LANGS NAS
THAL MO SBYAR BA BTUD DE, SANGS RGYAS KYI MDO SDE 'DI BDAG CAG LA
GTAD DU GSOL, ZHES GSOL TO, ,DE'I TSE


@313B TSE DANG LDAN PA KUN DGA' BOS, 'DI SKAD CES GSOL TO, ,BCOM
LDAN 'DAS, MDO SDE 'DI'I MTSAN CI ZHES BGYI, JI LTAR YONGS SU
GZUNG, BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS KUN DGA' BO

LA BKA' STZAL PA, MDO SDE 'DI'I MING DGE BA'I DNGOS PO KUN BSDU
BA ZHES KYANG BYA, THABS MKHAS PA CHEN PO ZHES KYANG BYA, DGONGS
PA DAM PA'I SPYOD PA ZHES KYANG BYA, SANGS RGYAS DRIN

LAN BSAB PA ZHES KYANG BYA'O, ,BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS KUN DGA' BO
DANG, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' SEMS DPA' CHEN PO RNAMS LA 'DI SKAD
CES BKA' STZAL TO, ,KHYED RNAMS JI LTAR

BSTAN PA BZHIN DU NAN TAN DU SPYOD CIG ,SANGS RGYAS KYIS YONGS SU
GDAMS PA'I LE'U 'DI BSTAN PA'I TSE, NYAN THOS BDUN KHRI NYIS
STONG GIS, BLA NA MED PA'I BYANG CHUB TU SEMS BSKYED

PAR GYUR TO, ,GZHAN YANG, LHA DANG, KLU DANG, GNOD SBYIN DANG,
DRI ZA DANG, MI'AM CI DANG, LTO 'PHYE CHEN PO DANG, MI DANG, MI
MA YIN PA DANG, DE LA SOGS PA THAMS CAD SANGS

RGYAS KYIS GSUNGS PA LA RJES SU YI RANGS BAR GYUR TO, ,THABS
MKHAS PA CHEN PO SANGS RGYAS DRIN LAN BSAB PA'I MDO LAS, NYE BAR
BSNYEN PA'I LE'U ZHES BYA STE DGU PA'O,, ,,

THABS MKHAS PA CHEN PO SANGS RGYAS DRIN LAN BSAB PA ZHES BYA BA'I
MDO RDZOGS SO,, ,,RGYA NAG LA SA BOD DU 'GYUR BA LA 'GYUR GSAR
BCAD MA BYAS PA'O,, ,,
